                   Champions League quarter-final draw
                  </h2>
                 </header>

                  Bayern and Paris will meet in a repeat of last season's UEFA Champions League final.

                  <h2 class="article--title">
                   Quarter-finals start Wednesday
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  Lyon face Paris, Chelsea meet Wolfsburg, Manchester City play Barcelona and Bayern take on Rosengård from Wednesday.
                 </div>
                </div>
               </article>
              </a>

                  <h2 class="article--title">
                   Croatia and Slovenia legends turn out in force for Petrinja
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  President Aleksander Čeferin joined an all-star cast as Slovenian legends overcame their Croatian counterparts in a charity game.

                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  Bosnia and Herzegovina, Azerbaijan, Croatia, Italy, Russia and Spain have joined hosts Netherlands; the groups end in April.
                 </div>
                </div>
               </article>
              </a>
             </div>
            </div>

                <div class="article--content">
                 <header class="article--header">
                  <span class="live-indicator">
                   Live
                  </span>
                  <h2 class="article--title">
                   Play-offs: 9 and 13 April
                  </h2>
                 </header>
                 <div class="article--summary">
                  Ukraine face Northern Ireland, Portugal take on Russia and Czech Republic play Switzerland for the last three finals spots.
                 </div>
                </div>
               </article>
              </a>

The association club coefficient or country rankings take into account the results of all clubs from each association and are used to determine the number of entries an association is granted for forthcoming seasons.
